WITHOUT KNOWING THE SPECIFIC DATA WHICH YOU
REQUIRE FROM YOUR CLIENTS, IT IS DIFFICULT TO
DETERMINE WHICH WOULD BE THE MOST APPROPRIATE
MESSAGE TYPE TO BE USED, ALTHOUGH THE CHOICE IS
IN ANY CASE LIMITED.
IN ADDITION TO THE MT 553 INSTRUCTION TO A
CUSTODIAN WHICH YOU MENTIONED, YOU MIGHT ALSO
CONSIDER THE MT 500 ORDER TO BUY.
YOU NEED TO CONSIDER HOW AND WHERE YOU WOULD ROUTE
THE MESSAGE ON RECEIPT, AND WHETHER THE MT 553 IS
OR MIGHT BE USED ALREADY TO INSTRUCT OTHER TYPES
OF OPERATIONS HANDLED BY DIFFERENT AREAS IN THE
BANK.
THE MT 553 HAS A SLIGHT ADVANTAGE IN THAT IT
CONTAINS A LARGE NARRATIVE FIELD, MISSING IN
THE MT 500, THE USE OF WHICH COULD BE DEFINED
BILATERALLY.  THE MT 500, ON THE OTHER HAND,
ALLOWS PROPRIETARY CODE WORDS TO BE USED IN FIELD
23.  IN TERMS OF THE ROLE YOU ARE PLAYING, IT
SEEMS THAT YOU ARE PERFORMING MORE THE ROLE OF
BROKER THAN CUSTODIAN, AND AS SUCH I WOULD
RECOMMEND THE MT 500, BUT THIS IS SUBJECTIVE.
IF YOU NEED FURTHER INFO, FEEL FREE TO CONTACT ME
(PHONE +32 2 655 3266 OR FAX +32 2 655 3801).
BEST REGARDS, STANDARDS MANAGER
